Bf  the  term  idea,  I  mean  whatever  is  the  object

whatever  it  is  which  the  mind  can  be  employed  about

perceived,  and  reflecled  on  by  in,  we  may  call  Reflec-

Of  Knowledge  in  General*

§   I.

SInce  the  mind  in  all  its  thoughts  and  reafonings,

h  alone  it  does  or  can  contemplate  ;  it  i.;  evident

on of  the  connexion  and  agreement,  cr  difagrccrnent  and
repugnancy  of  any  tf  our  ideas  :  Where  this  percepti-
on is,  there  is  knowledge  ;  aod  where  it  is  not,  there,
though  we  fancy,  guefs,  or  believe,  yet  we  always
